The core issue is becoming clear: DGF and AbsReturn sit at config positions 7 and 8, but in the actual column layout they're at 7 and 8 between Annuities (column 6) and Insurance (column 9)—so the algorithm never identifies them as unmatched because they don't fall into the gaps between the pairs being checked.

The solution is to flip the approach entirely: instead of iterating through config pairs, I should sort all identified anchors by their actual column positions, then scan for unidentified columns that fall between consecutive anchors in that column-sorted order. This way I'm working directly in the space where the data actually lives, rather than trying to map config order onto column order.

For the specific case at hand, when I look at the anchors sorted by column position, I can see there's a gap between Annuities and Insurance with two empty columns that need to be filled. The unidentified series in that range should map to those gap columns based on their config definition order.

Now I'm refining the algorithm: I'll sort the identified anchors by their column index, then for each consecutive pair, identify any gaps between them and check if the count of unidentified series falling within that range matches the gap count. If it does, I can assign them in order. two anchor series

def_min = min(def_a, def_b), def_max = max(def_a, def_b)
unid = [codes_in_order[j] for j in range(def_min+1, def_max) if codes_in_order[j] not in code_to_col]
If len(unid) == len(gaps): assign unid → gaps (in config order → ascending column order)

# PPFPB Runbook — Claude Working Context

## Project Summary

Extract 19 data series from annual PPF Purple Book PDFs (pension fund asset allocation).
Pipeline: `config.py` → `scraper.py` → `extractor.py` → `file_generator.py` → `orchestrator.py` → `main.py`

**Current phase: testing `test_extraction.py` against all 5 PDFs before rewriting `extractor.py`.**
The user explicitly requires near-complete extraction accuracy confirmed in the test harness BEFORE touching `extractor.py`.

---

## File Locations

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `test_extraction.py` | Test harness — all logic changes go here first |
| `extractor.py` | Production extractor — DO NOT modify until testing is complete |
| `config.py` | Series definitions, paths, NA config |
| `Master_Data/Master_PPFPB_DATA.csv` | Ground truth reference data |
| `debug/<year>/` | camelot debug CSVs saved per run |
| `Project_information/` | Source PDFs + screenshots |

### PDF files
```
Project_information/Pension-Protection-Fund-Purple-Book-2025-accessible.pdf
Project_information/PPF-The-Purple-Book-2024.pdf
Project_information/PPF-The-Purple-Book-2023.pdf
Project_information/PPF_PurpleBook_2022.pdf
Project_information/PPF_PurpleBook_2021.pdf
```

---

## 19 Series Being Extracted

Defined in `config.SERIES_DEFINITIONS` — **order never changes**.

### Section: `asset_allocation` (11 series) — Config Definition Order
| Config Pos | Series Code (suffix) | Description |
|-----------|---------------------|-------------|
| 0 | `...LISTEDANDPRIVATEEQUITIES...` | Equities |
| 1 | `...BONDS...ACTUALALLOCATION...` | Bonds |
| 2 | `...ALTERNATIVES...` | Other Investments |
| 3 | `...REALESTATE...` | Property |
| 4 | `...CASH...` | Cash and Deposits |
| 5 | `...INSURANCE...` | Insurance policies |
| 6 | `...HEDGEFUNDS...` | Hedge Funds |
| 7 | `...DEVIGROWFUND...` | Diversified growth funds (DGF) |
| 8 | `...ABSRETURN...` | Absolute returns |
| 9 | `...ANNUITIES...` | Annuities |
| 10 | `...OTHER...ACTUALALLOCATION...` | Miscellaneous |

### Section: `bond_splits` (3 series)
Government fixed interest, Corporate fixed interest, Index-linked

### Section: `equity_splits` (5 series)
UK quoted, Overseas quoted, Developed markets, Emerging markets, Unquoted/Private

---

## Extraction Strategy

1. **pdfplumber** — find the page containing each section using keyword matching
2. **camelot** (stream flavor, `edge_tol=50`) — extract raw tables from those pages
3. **Decoder ring** — match prior-year master values against table cells (±0.15 tolerance) to identify which column = which series (no hardcoded column indices, no header parsing)
4. **Gap-fill** — for new series with no prior reference years, infer position from bracketing anchor columns
5. **Extract** target year row using confirmed column map

---

## Current Test Status (as of last session)

Run command: `PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8 python test_extraction.py`
Single year: `PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8 python test_extraction.py 2025`
Strip mode (simulate fresh run): `PYTHONIOENCODING=utf-8 python test_extraction.py 2023 strip`

| PDF Year | Series Extracted | Accuracy vs Master | Notes |
|----------|-----------------|-------------------|-------|
| 2025 | 17/17 (maybe 19/19 after equity fix) | 100% (17/17) | Fully working |
| 2024 | 16/17 | 94% | 1 structural diff (Corp FI combined vs split) — NOT a code bug |
| 2023 | **19/19** | 7/17 (41%) | Low accuracy is RESTATEMENT, not code bug — see below |
| 2022 | 15/15 | 100% | Fully working |
| 2021 | 15/15 | 100% | Fully working |

**NOTE:** The 2023 accuracy of 41% is expected and acceptable. The 2023 PDF contains original (unrestated) values. The master holds values updated from later PDFs. Diffs of 0.4–4.3 percentage points are restatement differences, not extraction errors.

**NOTE:** The 2024 Corp FI mismatch (extracted=35.0, master=27.7, diff=7.3) is a structural change. The 2024 PDF still uses the combined "Corporate fixed-interest" column (35.0%). The 2025 PDF split this into "Corporate public markets" (27.7%) + "Corporate private debt" (7.3%). The master stores 27.7 from the 2025 PDF. This is correct behaviour — not fixable.

---

## All Bugs Fixed in test_extraction.py

### Fix 1: PAGE_KEYWORDS — page detection
Old keyword `'weighted average asset allocation in total assets'` failed on 2021 PDF.
New keywords match all years:
```python
PAGE_KEYWORDS = {
    'asset_allocation': ['cash and deposits', 'annuities'],
    'bond_splits':      ['bond split', 'index-linked'],
    'equity_splits':    ['uk quoted', 'overseas quoted'],
}
```

### Fix 2: Minimum years threshold in find_pages
Require ≥4 distinct data years on a page to avoid false positives on executive-summary pages that mention only 1–2 years in narrative text. The 2023 bond_splits page was being incorrectly matched on page 6 without this.
```python
years_on_page = set(re.findall(r'\b20(?:0[6-9]|1[0-9]|2[0-9])\b', text))
if len(years_on_page) < 4:
    continue
```

### Fix 3: find_year_rows — year must start the cell
Old code used `re.search` and picked up `2023` from header cells like `(tier 1 only from 2023)`.
New code uses `re.match` (year must be at START of cell string):
```python
m = re.match(r'^(20\d{2})', s)
```
Also scans ALL columns (not just col 0) to handle the 2021 combined bond/equity table where col 0 is sidebar text and year is in col 1.

### Fix 4: _split_embedded_values — strips annotation before values
Cell like `"2023 restated*\n7\n.6%\n..."` was being split into `["restated*", "7.6%", ...]`. The `"restated*"` got inserted as col 1, shifting all subsequent values one column to the right.
Fix: strip any leading non-value annotation text:
```python
while values and not _is_value_fragment(values[0]):
    values.pop(0)
```

### Fix 5: normalize_rows — expands squished col 0
camelot sometimes merges an entire year row into col 0: `"2024\n6.6%\n1.4%\n41.7%\n..."`.
normalize_rows detects this (≥2 value fragments in col 0 after the year) and expands them into separate columns.
This was needed for 2024 equity_splits.

### Fix 6: _fill_positional_gaps — rewritten to work in COLUMN INDEX SPACE
**This is the most important fix (completed in the last session).**

#### The Problem
The old algorithm sorted anchors by **config definition index** and looked for gaps between consecutive config-order pairs. This failed for `asset_allocation` in 2023 because:
- PDF column order: `Annuities(col6), DGF(col7), AbsReturn(col8), Insurance(col9)`
- Config definition order: `Insurance(def5), Hedge(def6), DGF(def7), AbsReturn(def8), Annuities(def9)`
- The pair `(Hedge=col10, Annuities=col6)` has `col_b < col_a`, so `range(col_a+1, col_b)` = empty — no gap detected

#### The Fix
Sort anchors by **column index**. For each consecutive column pair, find unidentified series whose config positions fall **between** the two anchors' config positions (using `min`/`max` to handle non-monotonic PDF vs config ordering):

```python
def _fill_positional_gaps(col_map, series_list):
    if not col_map:
        return col_map

    codes_in_order = [code for code, _ in series_list]
    code_to_col    = {code: idx for idx, code in col_map.items()}

    # Sort identified anchors by COLUMN INDEX (not definition index)
    anchors = sorted(
        [(col, codes_in_order.index(code), code)
         for col, code in col_map.items()
         if code in codes_in_order],
        key=lambda x: x[0]
    )

    if len(anchors) < 2:
        return col_map

    for k in range(len(anchors) - 1):
        col_a, def_a, _ = anchors[k]
        col_b, def_b, _ = anchors[k + 1]
        # col_a < col_b guaranteed since sorted by column index

        gaps = [c for c in range(col_a + 1, col_b) if c not in col_map]
        if not gaps:
            continue

        # Use min/max so non-monotonic config vs column ordering is handled
        def_min = min(def_a, def_b)
        def_max = max(def_a, def_b)
        unid = [codes_in_order[j]
                for j in range(def_min + 1, def_max)
                if codes_in_order[j] not in code_to_col]

        if len(unid) == len(gaps):
            for code, col in zip(unid, gaps):
                col_map[col] = code
                code_to_col[code] = col

    return col_map
```

#### Verified Correct For
- **equity_splits 2023**: UK(col1/def0), OS(col2/def1), Unquoted(col5/def4) → pair (col2,col5): gaps=[3,4], unid=[Dev(def2),Emg(def3)] → Dev→col3, Emg→col4 ✓
- **asset_allocation 2023**: pair (col6=Annuities/def9, col9=Insurance/def5): def_min=5, def_max=9, unid=[DGF(def7),AbsReturn(def8)], gaps=[7,8] → DGF→col7, AbsReturn→col8 ✓
- No false fills for earlier years where DGF/AbsReturn columns don't exist in the PDF ✓

---

## 2023 PDF Asset Allocation — Column Layout (Critical Reference)

From `debug/2023/asset_allocation_p24_t0.csv`:

| Col Index | Header in PDF | Config Def Pos | Series |
|-----------|--------------|----------------|--------|
| 0 | Year | — | Year label |
| 1 | Equities | def0 | Equities |
| 2 | Bonds | def1 | Bonds |
| 3 | Other investments | def2 | Other Investments |
| 4 | Cash and deposits | def4 | Cash (NOTE: before Property) |
| 5 | Property | def3 | Property (NOTE: after Cash) |
| 6 | Annuities | def9 | Annuities (NOTE: def9 but col6) |
| 7 | Diversified growth funds | def7 | DGF — **new in 2023, no prior ref years** |
| 8 | Absolute returns | def8 | AbsReturn — **new in 2023, no prior ref years** |
| 9 | Insurance policies | def5 | Insurance |
| 10 | Hedge funds | def6 | Hedge Funds |
| 11 | Miscellaneous | def10 | Miscellaneous |

The 2023 PDF shows `n/a` for Insurance and Hedge in the 2023 row (columns 9 and 10).
The 2023 PDF shows `n/a` for DGF and AbsReturn in ALL rows PRIOR to 2023 — that is why the decoder ring cannot match them from reference years and gap-fill is required.

## Key Technical Rules (Do Not Break)

1. **camelot stream flavor only** — never use lattice
2. **No hardcoded column indices** — decoder ring only
3. **No header text parsing** — value matching only
4. **Tolerance is ±0.15 percentage points** (`_TOLERANCE = 0.15`)
5. **NA_OUTPUT_VALUE = 'NA'** (string, not None) — from config
6. **DEBUG_CSV = True** in extractor.py writes debug CSVs to `debug/<year>/`
7. **Master CSV structure**: row 0 = series codes, row 1 = descriptions, rows 2+ = year data
8. **Target year logic**: `target_year = max(master_years) + 1`; falls back to latest year in table if not found

---

## Known Permanent Limitations (Not Code Bugs)

1. **2023 restatement**: Master holds restated 2023 values from later PDFs. The 2023 PDF itself has original values. Diffs of 0.4–4.3pp are expected when extracting directly from the 2023 PDF.

2. **2024 Corporate FI split**: 2024 PDF has combined Corp FI = 35.0%. 2025 PDF splits into Corp public markets (27.7%) + Corp private debt (7.3%). Master stores 27.7 from 2025. Diff of 7.3 when testing 2024 PDF — structural change, not fixable.

3. **DGF and AbsReturn always NA for pre-2023 PDFs**: These categories didn't exist. Code correctly returns NA for them when extracting from 2021/2022 PDFs.

4. **Insurance and Hedge show NA in 2023 PDF for the 2023 row**: The 2023 PDF reports n/a for these two categories specifically for the year 2023. Correct behaviour.
